Conditions</a><span data-identity="divider" class="font-medium">/</span></div><span data-identity="breadcrumb-current-page" class="uppercase text-gray-800 inline-block font-semibold">Amyotrophic Lateral Sclerosis (ALS)</span></div><div data-identity="sticky-leaderboard-ad"><div data-identity="leaderboard-ad" class="hidden bp1100:flex justify-center my-rem24px "><div class="relative"><span data-identity="side-ad-label" class="absolute uppercase text-rem10px leading-rem16px text-center w-[100px] text-gray-800 top-[37px] left-[-57px] rotate-[-90deg]">Advertisement</span><div data-identity="ad-slot" id="leaderboard_728x90" class="ad-reset min-w-[728px] !min-h-[90px] flex bg-gray-300"></div><span data-identity="side-ad-label" class="absolute uppercase text-rem10px leading-rem16px text-center w-[100px] text-gray-800 top-[37px] right-[-57px] rotate-[90deg]">Advertisement</span></div></div></div><div data-identity="leaderboard-ad-page-header-placeholder" class="hidden "></div><h1 data-identity="headline" class="text-gray-900 font-black leading-rem44px text-rem40px bp600:text-rem48px bp600:leading-rem52px max-w-headerWide">Amyotrophic Lateral Sclerosis (ALS)</h1><div data-identity="horizontal-bar" class="w-[40px] h-[5px] bg-brandBlue-500 mt-rem40px"></div><div class="mt-rem48px"><p data-identity="intro-text" class="font-normal text-rem19px leading-rem32px text-gray-800 bp900:leading-rem34px max-w-body undefined">ALS (amyotrophic lateral sclerosis) is a neurodegenerative condition that affects how nerve cells communicate with your muscles. It leads to muscle weakness that gets worse over time. Symptoms can affect how you move, speak and breathe. ALS treatment includes therapies and medications to manage symptoms and slow the progression of the disease.</p></div></div></section><div class="container mt-rem48px mb-rem64px bp900:mb-rem88px"><div data-identity="article-sidebar" class="hidden bp900:block bp900:pl-rem48px bp900:row-span-2 bp900:w-1/3 bp900:float-right"><div style="height:auto"><div class="sticky pt-rem16px mb-rem32px" style="top:0px"><div data-identity="billboard-ad" class="hidden bp1100:flex max-w-[400px] min-w-[300px] m-auto items-center justify-center bg-gray-300 pt-rem16px pb-[2.25rem] mb-rem32px"><div class="max-w-[300px] mx-auto"><p class="text-gray-800 uppercase text-rem10px leading-rem16px mx-auto w-fit">Advertisement</p><div class="hidden bp1100:flex flex-col items-center justify-center"><div data-identity="ad-slot" id="billboard_300x250" class="ad-reset w-[300px] !min-h-[250px] flex bg-gray-300"></div><div data-identity="ad-policy" class="text-rem13px text-gray-900 pt-rem16px max-w-[300px] mx-auto"><p>Cleveland Clinic is a non-profit academic medical center. Advertising on our site helps support our mission. data-identity="main-article-content" class="bp900:pr-rem48px bp900:pt-[1px] bp900:border-r bp900:border-gray-400 bp900:border-1 bp900:w-2/3"><div><div data-identity="article-section" id="overview" class="scroll-mt-[112px]"><h2 data-identity="headline" class="text-gray-900 font-bold leading-rem34px text-rem32px bp600:text-rem40px bp600:leading-rem44px mt-rem56px mb-rem16px break-words">Overview</h2><div data-identity="rich-text" class=""><h3 data-identity="headline" class="text-gray-900 font-bold leading-rem30px text-rem25px bp600:text-rem32px bp600:leading-rem38px mt-rem32px mb-rem16px break-words ">What is ALS?</h3><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">ALS, or amyotrophic lateral sclerosis, is a <a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/diseases/24976-neurodegenerative-diseases" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition">neurodegenerative condition</a> that affects the nerve cells (neurons) in your <a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/body/22638-brain" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition">brain</a> and <a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/body/21946-spinal-cord" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition">spinal cord</a>. It targets your motor neurons. These regulate voluntary muscle movements (like the ones you use to talk, chew and move your arms and legs) and breathing.</p><div data-identity="billboard-ad" class="flex bp1100:hidden max-w-[400px] min-w-[300px] m-auto items-center justify-center bg-gray-300 pt-rem16px pb-[2.25rem] my-rem32px "><div class="max-w-[300px] mx-auto"><p class="text-gray-800 uppercase text-rem10px leading-rem16px mx-auto w-fit">Advertisement</p><div class="flex bp1100:hidden flex-col items-center justify-center"><div data-identity="ad-slot" id="billboard_300x250_mobile" class="ad-reset w-[300px] !min-h-[250px] flex bg-gray-300"></div><div data-identity="ad-policy" class="text-rem13px text-gray-900 pt-rem16px max-w-[300px] mx-auto"><p>Cleveland Clinic is a non-profit academic medical center. Advertising on our site helps support our mission. We do not endorse non-Cleveland Clinic products or services.<!-- --> <a data-identity="ad-policy-link" href="https://health.clevelandclinic.org/advertising" target="_blank" class="text-blue-600 hover:text-blue-800 transition underline" rel="noreferrer">Policy</a></p></div></div></div></div><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Your neurons communicate with your <a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/body/muscles" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition">muscles</a> to tell them to move. ALS disrupts the communication, like bad phone reception. The messages sent from neurons to muscles break up and dont get through clearly, which eventually causes the call to end. As a result of this poor connection, neurons cant take any new calls.</p><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Symptoms of ALS progressively get worse over time. You might notice muscle weakness and muscle twitching that affects your ability to walk independently, reach for objects, chew food and talk. ALS eventually causes your muscles to waste away (<a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/diseases/22310-muscle-atrophy" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition">atrophy</a>). Atrophy can interfere with your ability to breathe and lead to life-threatening outcomes.</p><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Although theres no cure for ALS, the treatments are constantly improving. The right combination of treatments can help slow the progression of the disease and improve your quality of life.</p><h4 data-identity="headline" class="text-gray-900 font-bold leading-rem24px text-rem20px bp600:text-rem25px bp600:leading-rem30px mt-rem32px mb-rem16px break-words ">Why is ALS called Lou Gehrigs disease?</h4><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">ALS was formerly known as Lou Gehrigs disease. Lou Gehrig was a famous baseball player in the 1920s and 1930s who had ALS.</p><h4 data-identity="headline" class="text-gray-900 font-bold leading-rem24px text-rem20px bp600:text-rem25px bp600:leading-rem30px mt-rem32px mb-rem16px break-words ">What are the types of ALS?</h4><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">There are two types of ALS based on their cause:</p><ul data-identity="unordered-list" class="my-rem16px mx-0 pl-[1.25rem] list-disc marker:text-brandBlue-500 marker:pl-rem24px "><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px "><strong>Sporadic ALS</strong>: An estimated 90% of all ALS cases are sporadic. This means that the condition happens randomly. It isnt inherited (passed from biological parents to children).</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px "><strong>Familial ALS</strong>: About 10% of ALS cases are familial. A gene change (<a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/body/23095-genetic-mutations-in-humans" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition">mutation</a>) causes it. You inherit the gene change from one or both of your biological parents during conception.</li></ul><div data-identity="billboard-ad" class="flex bp1100:hidden max-w-[400px] min-w-[300px] m-auto items-center justify-center bg-gray-300 pt-rem16px pb-[3.125rem] my-rem32px "><div class="max-w-[300px] mx-auto"><p class="text-gray-800 uppercase text-rem10px leading-rem16px mx-auto w-fit">Advertisement</p><div class="flex bp1100:hidden flex-col items-center justify-center"><div data-identity="ad-slot" id="billboard2_300x250_mobile" class="ad-reset w-[300px] !min-h-[250px] flex bg-gray-300"></div></div></div></div><h4 data-identity="headline" class="text-gray-900 font-bold leading-rem24px text-rem20px bp600:text-rem25px bp600:leading-rem30px mt-rem32px mb-rem16px break-words ">How common is ALS?</h4><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">An estimated 5,000 people in the United States receive an ALS diagnosis each year.</p><div data-identity="native-ad-desktop" class="hidden bp1100:block "><div data-identity="native-ad-slot" id="native_desktop" class="ad-reset my-rem64px empty:my-0 *:last:bg-gradient-to-r *:last:bg-[32px] *:last:bg-no-repeat bp1100:w-full bp1100:overflow-hidden *:last:from-blue-050 *:last:to-blue-050"></div></div></div></div></div><div><div data-identity="article-section" id="symptoms-and-causes" class="scroll-mt-[112px]"><h2 data-identity="headline" class="text-gray-900 font-bold leading-rem34px text-rem32px bp600:text-rem40px bp600:leading-rem44px mt-rem56px mb-rem16px break-words">Symptoms and Causes</h2><figure data-identity="figure" itemProp="" itemType="" class="bg-gray-300 bp600:bg-transparent bp900:mt-rem8px bp900:pl-rem16px bp900:pr-0 py-rem16px px-rem24px bp900:max-w-[50%] bp900:float-right bp900:w-[50%]"><img data-identity="featured-image" class="w-full bp600:border-4 bp600:border-gray-300" src="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/-/scassets/images/org/health/articles/16729-amyotrophic-lateral-sclerosis-als" alt="Common symptoms of ALS caused by motor neuron damage include muscle weakness, tremors and speech challenges" loading="lazy"/><figcaption data-identity="figure-caption" itemProp="description" class="text-gray-900 text-rem13px leading-rem20px mt-rem12px">ALS causes symptoms that progressively get worse over time.</figcaption></figure><div data-identity="rich-text" class=""><h3 data-identity="headline" class="text-gray-900 font-bold leading-rem30px text-rem25px bp600:text-rem32px bp600:leading-rem38px mt-rem32px mb-rem16px break-words ">What are the symptoms of ALS?</h3><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">ALS symptoms include:</p><ul data-identity="unordered-list" class="my-rem16px mx-0 pl-[1.25rem] list-disc marker:text-brandBlue-500 marker:pl-rem24px "><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Muscle weakness (arms, legs and neck).</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px "><a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/diseases/15466-muscle-spasms" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition">Muscle cramps</a>.</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px "><a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/symptoms/15301-myoclonus-muscle-twitch" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition">Twitching</a> (fasciculations) in your hands, feet, shoulder and/or tongue.</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px "><a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/symptoms/25147-muscle-stiffness" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition">Stiff muscles</a> (spasticity).</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Speech challenges (slurring words, trouble forming words).</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Drooling.</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Involuntary emotional expressions (like laughing or crying).</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px "><a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/symptoms/21206-fatigue" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition">Fatigue</a>.</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Trouble swallowing (<a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/symptoms/21195-dysphagia-difficulty-swallowing" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition">dysphagia</a>).</li></ul><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">These symptoms start out mild and get more severe. The speed at which symptoms progress varies from person to person.</p><h4 data-identity="headline" class="text-gray-900 font-bold leading-rem24px text-rem20px bp600:text-rem25px bp600:leading-rem30px mt-rem32px mb-rem16px break-words ">ALS early symptoms</h4><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">The first symptoms of ALS you might notice are muscle weakness and stiffness. These symptoms can affect your:</p><ul data-identity="unordered-list" class="my-rem16px mx-0 pl-[1.25rem] list-disc marker:text-brandBlue-500 marker:pl-rem24px "><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Arms and legs (limb onset).</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Speech and swallowing (bulbar onset).</li></ul><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">It may be more difficult for you to do routine things, like writing your name or buttoning your shirt. You might need more time to eat meals than usual.</p><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">No matter where the symptoms begin, theyll spread to other parts of your body.</p><h4 data-identity="headline" class="text-gray-900 font-bold leading-rem24px text-rem20px bp600:text-rem25px bp600:leading-rem30px mt-rem32px mb-rem16px break-words ">Severe ALS symptoms</h4><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Severe ALS symptoms can include:</p><ul data-identity="unordered-list" class="my-rem16px mx-0 pl-[1.25rem] list-disc marker:text-brandBlue-500 marker:pl-rem24px "><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px "><a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/symptoms/16942-dyspnea" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition">Shortness of breath</a> and difficulty breathing.</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Inability to stand, walk or get out of bed independently.</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Weight loss and trouble maintaining a healthy weight.</li></ul><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">If you experience severe symptoms, contact a healthcare provider. If you have trouble breathing, contact emergency services right away.</p><div data-identity="native-ad-mobile" class="mx-auto relative bp1100:hidden bp900:overflow-hidden bp900:w-full"><div data-identity="native-ad-bg" class="absolute bp900:hidden z-[-1] w-full h-full [border-image:conic-gradient(theme(colors.blue.050)_0_0)_fill_0/4rem_0_2rem/2rem_100vw]"></div><div data-identity="native-ad-slot" id="native_mobile" class="ad-reset empty:pb-0 mb-rem56px empty:mb-0 *:last:!mt-rem56px *:last:!mb-rem32px pb-rem32px *:bp900:last:bg-gradient-to-r *:bp900:last:from-blue-050 *:bp900:last:to-blue-050 *:bp900:last:bg-[0_32px] *:bp900:last:bg-no-repeat *:bp900:last:!pb-rem64px bp900:pb-0"></div></div><h3 data-identity="headline" class="text-gray-900 font-bold leading-rem30px text-rem25px bp600:text-rem32px bp600:leading-rem38px mt-rem32px mb-rem16px break-words ">What causes ALS?</h3><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Researchers dont know what causes ALS. They believe its a combination of the following factors:</p><ul data-identity="unordered-list" class="my-rem16px mx-0 pl-[1.25rem] list-disc marker:text-brandBlue-500 marker:pl-rem24px "><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px "><strong>Genetics</strong>: Changes or variants in certain <a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/body/23064-dna-genes--chromosomes" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition">genes</a> may cause ALS in up to 70% of familial cases and 5% to 10% of sporadic cases. There are more than 40 genes related to ALS. The most common affected genes include the <em>C9orf72</em>, <em>SOD1</em>, <em>TARDBP</em> and <em>FUS</em> genes that regulate how neurons function.</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px "><strong>Environment</strong>: Exposure to certain toxic substances (<a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/diseases/11312-lead-poisoning" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition">lead</a> or <a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/diseases/23420-mercury-poisoning" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition">mercury</a>), viruses or physical trauma may cause ALS.</li></ul><h4 data-identity="headline" class="text-gray-900 font-bold leading-rem24px text-rem20px bp600:text-rem25px bp600:leading-rem30px mt-rem32px mb-rem16px break-words ">Is ALS genetic?</h4><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Yes, some types of ALS are genetic. You can inherit genetic changes that cause ALS from your biological parents. Inherited ALS isnt common, though. Sometimes, genetic changes happen randomly, without a history in your biological family.</p><h4 data-identity="headline" class="text-gray-900 font-bold leading-rem24px text-rem20px bp600:text-rem25px bp600:leading-rem30px mt-rem32px mb-rem16px break-words ">What are the risk factors for ALS?</h4><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Risk factors for ALS include:</p><ul data-identity="unordered-list" class="my-rem16px mx-0 pl-[1.25rem] list-disc marker:text-brandBlue-500 marker:pl-rem24px "><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px "><strong>Age</strong>: Youre most likely to develop symptoms between ages 55 and 75.</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px "><strong>Race and ethnicity</strong>: White (non-Hispanic) people are most likely to get ALS.</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px "><a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/articles/sex-recorded-at-birth" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition"><strong>Sex</strong></a>: For cases that occur before age 55, men are at higher risk.</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px "><strong>Veterans</strong>: Military veterans may be at higher risk. Researchers suggest its from environmental exposure (toxins or pesticides) or physical trauma.</li></ul><h3 data-identity="headline" class="text-gray-900 font-bold leading-rem30px text-rem25px bp600:text-rem32px bp600:leading-rem38px mt-rem32px mb-rem16px break-words ">What are the complications of ALS?</h3><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">ALS will shorten your life expectancy as symptoms get more severe. Learning about this diagnosis and dealing with it every day can take a toll on your mental health. You may feel overwhelmed, lost, hopeless or stressed. As a result, many people diagnosed with ALS also develop <a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/diseases/9290-depression" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition">depression</a> and <a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/diseases/9536-anxiety-disorders" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition">anxiety</a>.</p><div data-identity="billboard-ad" class="flex bp1100:hidden max-w-[400px] min-w-[300px] m-auto items-center justify-center bg-gray-300 pt-rem16px pb-[3.125rem] my-rem32px "><div class="max-w-[300px] mx-auto"><p class="text-gray-800 uppercase text-rem10px leading-rem16px mx-auto w-fit">Advertisement</p><div class="flex bp1100:hidden flex-col items-center justify-center"><div data-identity="ad-slot" id="billboard3_300x250_mobile" class="ad-reset w-[300px] !min-h-[250px] flex bg-gray-300"></div></div></div></div><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">It isnt easy to manage ALS on your own. While youll be working with a number of providers for your physical health, make sure you take care of your emotional health as well. Talk to your care team or a mental health provider for help.</p></div></div></div><div><div data-identity="article-section" id="diagnosis-and-tests" class="scroll-mt-[112px]"><h2 data-identity="headline" class="text-gray-900 font-bold leading-rem34px text-rem32px bp600:text-rem40px bp600:leading-rem44px mt-rem56px mb-rem16px break-words">Diagnosis and Tests</h2><div data-identity="rich-text" class=""><h3 data-identity="headline" class="text-gray-900 font-bold leading-rem30px text-rem25px bp600:text-rem32px bp600:leading-rem38px mt-rem32px mb-rem16px break-words ">How is ALS diagnosed?</h3><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Your healthcare provider will offer a <a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/diagnostics/17366-physical-examination" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition">physical exam</a>, <a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/diagnostics/22664-neurological-exam" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition">neurological exam</a> and testing to make an ALS diagnosis.</p><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">An ALS diagnosis doesnt happen immediately. Youll likely schedule several office visits to see your provider or referring physicians. Your provider will order multiple tests to learn more about your symptoms and how they affect your body. There are a lot of conditions that have similar symptoms to ALS, so multiple exams and testing are necessary for an accurate diagnosis.</p><h4 data-identity="headline" class="text-gray-900 font-bold leading-rem24px text-rem20px bp600:text-rem25px bp600:leading-rem30px mt-rem32px mb-rem16px break-words ">What tests diagnose ALS?</h4><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Youll need several tests to confirm an ALS diagnosis, including:</p><ul data-identity="unordered-list" class="my-rem16px mx-0 pl-[1.25rem] list-disc marker:text-brandBlue-500 marker:pl-rem24px "><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px "><a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/diagnostics/24508-blood-tests" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition">Blood tests</a>.</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px "><a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/diagnostics/17893-urinalysis" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition">Urine tests</a>.</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px "><a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/articles/4825-electromyograms" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition">Electromyogram</a> (EMG) to measure the electrical activity of your nerves and muscles.</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">A <a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/treatments/24821-nerve-conduction-study" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition">nerve conduction study </a>to test your nerves ability to send signals.</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px "><a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/diagnostics/4876-magnetic-resonance-imaging-mri" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition">Magnetic resonance imaging</a> (MRI) to look at your brain or spine for areas of damage.</li></ul><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Other tests cant diagnose ALS but can help rule out different conditions that may cause similar symptoms:</p><ul data-identity="unordered-list" class="my-rem16px mx-0 pl-[1.25rem] list-disc marker:text-brandBlue-500 marker:pl-rem24px "><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">A <a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/diagnostics/12544-lumbar-puncture-spinal-tap" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition">lumbar puncture</a>.</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Muscle and/or nerve <a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/diagnostics/15458-biopsy-overview" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition">biopsy</a>.</li></ul><div data-identity="billboard-ad" class="flex bp1100:hidden max-w-[400px] min-w-[300px] m-auto items-center justify-center bg-gray-300 pt-rem16px pb-[3.125rem] my-rem32px "><div class="max-w-[300px] mx-auto"><p class="text-gray-800 uppercase text-rem10px leading-rem16px mx-auto w-fit">Advertisement</p><div class="flex bp1100:hidden flex-col items-center justify-center"><div data-identity="ad-slot" id="billboard4_300x250_mobile" class="ad-reset w-[300px] !min-h-[250px] flex bg-gray-300"></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div><div data-identity="article-section" id="management-and-treatment" class="scroll-mt-[112px]"><h2 data-identity="headline" class="text-gray-900 font-bold leading-rem34px text-rem32px bp600:text-rem40px bp600:leading-rem44px mt-rem56px mb-rem16px break-words">Management and Treatment</h2><div data-identity="rich-text" class=""><h3 data-identity="headline" class="text-gray-900 font-bold leading-rem30px text-rem25px bp600:text-rem32px bp600:leading-rem38px mt-rem32px mb-rem16px break-words ">How is ALS treated?</h3><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">No treatment can reverse motor neuron damage. But treatment can help delay the progression of symptoms and improve your quality of life.</p><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Your care team might recommend the following treatments for ALS:</p><ul data-identity="unordered-list" class="my-rem16px mx-0 pl-[1.25rem] list-disc marker:text-brandBlue-500 marker:pl-rem24px "><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Medications.</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Therapies or rehabilitation.</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Nutritional support.</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Breathing support.</li></ul><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">You may need different types or more treatment options as the disease progresses. In addition, supportive care is available to meet your needs so you can live as comfortably and independently as possible for as long as possible.</p><h4 data-identity="headline" class="text-gray-900 font-bold leading-rem24px text-rem20px bp600:text-rem25px bp600:leading-rem30px mt-rem32px mb-rem16px break-words ">What medications treat ALS?</h4><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">There are four medications approved by the U.S. Food and Drug Administration (FDA) to treat ALS:</p><ul data-identity="unordered-list" class="my-rem16px mx-0 pl-[1.25rem] list-disc marker:text-brandBlue-500 marker:pl-rem24px "><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px "><a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/drugs/20937-riluzole-tablets" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition"><strong>Riluzole</strong></a> may help reduce damage to the motor neurons. It may extend survival by a few months. You can take this medication by mouth (orally).</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px "><a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/drugs/23656-edaravone-oral-suspension" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition"><strong>Edaravone</strong></a> can slow the decline in your muscle functioning. You can take this medication by mouth or a provider can administer it into a vein in your arm (intravenously). One form of this medication can be given through a feeding tube.</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px "><a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/drugs/24697-sodium-phenylbutyrate-taurursodiol-powder-for-suspension" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition"><strong>Sodium phenylbutyrate/taurursodiol</strong></a> can slow the progression of symptoms. This is an oral medication you can take by mouth.</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px "><strong>Tofersen</strong> can decrease some damage to neurons. This spinal injection can help if your provider finds a genetic change on the <em>SOD1</em> gene.</li></ul><div data-identity="billboard-ad" class="flex bp1100:hidden max-w-[400px] min-w-[300px] m-auto items-center justify-center bg-gray-300 pt-rem16px pb-[3.125rem] my-rem32px "><div class="max-w-[300px] mx-auto"><p class="text-gray-800 uppercase text-rem10px leading-rem16px mx-auto w-fit">Advertisement</p><div class="flex bp1100:hidden flex-col items-center justify-center"><div data-identity="ad-slot" id="billboard5_300x250_mobile" class="ad-reset w-[300px] !min-h-[250px] flex bg-gray-300"></div></div></div></div><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Other medications are available to manage your symptoms, like medications for muscle cramps, stiffness and excess saliva production, pain and mental health challenges.</p><h4 data-identity="headline" class="text-gray-900 font-bold leading-rem24px text-rem20px bp600:text-rem25px bp600:leading-rem30px mt-rem32px mb-rem16px break-words ">ALS therapies</h4><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Your provider might recommend different types of therapy or rehabilitation for ALS, including:</p><ul data-identity="unordered-list" class="my-rem16px mx-0 pl-[1.25rem] list-disc marker:text-brandBlue-500 marker:pl-rem24px "><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px "><strong>Physical therapy</strong>: The goal of physical therapy for ALS is to help you remain independent and safe. Gentle <a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/articles/7050-aerobic-exercise" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition">aerobic exercise</a>, such as walking or swimming, can strengthen muscles and improve your general health.</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px "><strong>Occupational therapy</strong>: Occupational therapy teaches you techniques and strategies for moving through your day. This is helpful if you need to use assistive devices, like a wheelchair, walker or braces. <a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/articles/24617-occupational-therapist" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition">Occupational therapists</a> can help you learn how to use these devices and move without feeling exhausted.</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px "><a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/treatments/22366-speech-therapy" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition"><strong>Speech therapy</strong></a>: Speech therapy provides strategies for safer swallowing, and communication training helps you maintain the ability to talk for as long as possible. Speech therapists can also teach you ways to communicate nonverbally. Even if you still have verbal abilities, you conserve energy with nonverbal communication.</li></ul><h4 data-identity="headline" class="text-gray-900 font-bold leading-rem24px text-rem20px bp600:text-rem25px bp600:leading-rem30px mt-rem32px mb-rem16px break-words ">Nutritional support for ALS</h4><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">It can be difficult to eat enough foods and drink enough fluids to meet your bodys needs with ALS. You may have trouble swallowing or eating certain foods, which may cause to you lose weight quickly and not get enough vitamins and minerals to support and strengthen your body.</p><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Dietitians can create a meal plan that avoids foods that are hard to swallow, and provides the right amount of calories, fiber and fluid for you. Nutritional counseling ensures you eat healthy, balanced meals. A nutritionist can also recommend other food options when swallowing becomes difficult.</p><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">At some point, you may need a <a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/treatments/21098-tube-feeding--enteral-nutrition" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition">feeding tube</a> to get the nutrition you need. A feeding tube also reduces the risk of choking and pneumonia. These complications come from accidentally inhaling liquid or food in your lungs.</p><h4 data-identity="headline" class="text-gray-900 font-bold leading-rem24px text-rem20px bp600:text-rem25px bp600:leading-rem30px mt-rem32px mb-rem16px break-words ">Breathing support for ALS</h4><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">As ALS progresses, you may find it hard to breathe. You might benefit from a type of breathing support called noninvasive ventilation (NIV). You get NIV through a mask that you wear over your nose and mouth. It can make breathing more comfortable. You might start using NIV only at night, but may need NIV full time later on.</p><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Eventually, you may need <a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/articles/15368-mechanical-ventilation" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition">mechanical ventilation</a>, which means using a respirator. This machine helps you breathe. It inflates and deflates your lungs.</p><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Let your care team know if you experience shortness of breath, especially when lying down or during physical activity. Theyll discuss options to make breathing easier.</p></div></div><div class="bp900:hidden mx-auto w-fit"><section data-identity="callout" class="flex flex-col justify-start max-w-[375px] bp600:max-w-[856px] bp900:max-w-[375px] bp600:gap-x-rem32px mt-rem48px bp900:mt-0 mb-rem32px"><div class="border-t-[5px] [width:40px] border-forestGreen-500 bp900:w-full"></div><div class="pt-rem16px pb-rem24px items-center flex align-middle"><div class="flex"><svg width="39" height="39" viewBox="0 0 39 39" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="flex-none mr-rem8px"><g><path data-identity="callout-logo-bottom" d="M8.33339 27.2665V20.6741H2.53202C0.94983 20.6741 -0.263184 21.9398 -0.263184 23.4693V35.9159C-0.263184 37.498 1.00257 38.7111 2.53202 38.7111H14.9786C16.5608 data-identity="callout-title" class="text-rem20px font-bold self-center leading-rem22px bp1100:leading-rem24px text-gray-900">Care at Cleveland Clinic</div></div></div><div data-identity="callout-links" class="justify-start pb-rem24px space-y-rem24px"><div data-identity="callout-detailed-link"><a data-identity="callout-link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/services/als-treatment" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 font-medium underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 hover:text-blue-800 transition">ALS Treatment</a></div><div data-identity="callout-detailed-link"><a data-identity="callout-link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/services/adult-cerebral-palsy-treatment#featured-provider-panel" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 font-medium underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 hover:text-blue-800 transition">Find a Doctor and Specialists</a></div><div data-identity="callout-detailed-link"><a data-identity="callout-link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/webappointment" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 font-medium underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 hover:text-blue-800 transition">Make an Appointment</a></div></div></section></div></div><div><div data-identity="article-section" id="prevention" class="scroll-mt-[112px]"><h2 data-identity="headline" class="text-gray-900 font-bold leading-rem34px text-rem32px bp600:text-rem40px bp600:leading-rem44px mt-rem56px mb-rem16px break-words">Prevention</h2><div data-identity="rich-text" class=""><h3 data-identity="headline" class="text-gray-900 font-bold leading-rem30px text-rem25px bp600:text-rem32px bp600:leading-rem38px mt-rem32px mb-rem16px break-words ">Can ALS be prevented?</h3><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Theres no proven way to prevent ALS. Research is ongoing to learn more about the causes and risk factors to help create prevention methods in the future.</p></div></div></div><div><div data-identity="article-section" id="outlook-prognosis" class="scroll-mt-[112px]"><h2 data-identity="headline" class="text-gray-900 font-bold leading-rem34px text-rem32px bp600:text-rem40px bp600:leading-rem44px mt-rem56px mb-rem16px break-words">Outlook / Prognosis</h2><div data-identity="rich-text" class=""><h3 data-identity="headline" class="text-gray-900 font-bold leading-rem30px text-rem25px bp600:text-rem32px bp600:leading-rem38px mt-rem32px mb-rem16px break-words ">What is the prognosis for ALS?</h3><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">The outlook for ALS is poor due to how the condition affects the functioning of your motor neurons. Your prognosis depends on how quickly motor neurons receive damage. No available treatment can reverse motor neuron damage. But your provider will offer options to help reduce the speed of symptom progression.</p><h4 data-identity="headline" class="text-gray-900 font-bold leading-rem24px text-rem20px bp600:text-rem25px bp600:leading-rem30px mt-rem32px mb-rem16px break-words ">How quickly does ALS progress?</h4><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">There isnt a set amount of time as to how quickly symptoms progress with ALS. They might progress faster without treatment. The speed can also vary by age, body composition at diagnosis (weight) and what symptoms you experience. Your provider may recommend taking certain medications that can help slow down disease progression.</p><h4 data-identity="headline" class="text-gray-900 font-bold leading-rem24px text-rem20px bp600:text-rem25px bp600:leading-rem30px mt-rem32px mb-rem16px break-words ">ALS life expectancy</h4><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">On average, the life expectancy after an ALS diagnosis is three to five years. An estimated 30% of people live five years or more and 10% to 20% live at least 10 years. Your life expectancy can vary from these statistics, so talk to your healthcare provider to learn more about your situation.</p><h4 data-identity="headline" class="text-gray-900 font-bold leading-rem24px text-rem20px bp600:text-rem25px bp600:leading-rem30px mt-rem32px mb-rem16px break-words ">ALS cure</h4><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Theres no available cure for ALS at this time.</p><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">If you have ALS, you may be interested in clinical trials. These are tests and studies on certain conditions to help researchers formulate prevention methods or create new treatment options. Doing so can help further understanding of the disease. As researchers gain more knowledge about ALS, they can learn more about causes and risk factors, too, which may pave the way to a cure in the future.</p></div></div></div><div><div data-identity="article-section" id="living-with" class="scroll-mt-[112px]"><h2 data-identity="headline" class="text-gray-900 font-bold leading-rem34px text-rem32px bp600:text-rem40px bp600:leading-rem44px mt-rem56px mb-rem16px break-words">Living With</h2><div data-identity="rich-text" class=""><h3 data-identity="headline" class="text-gray-900 font-bold leading-rem30px text-rem25px bp600:text-rem32px bp600:leading-rem38px mt-rem32px mb-rem16px break-words ">When should I see a healthcare provider?</h3><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Contact your healthcare provider if you:</p><ul data-identity="unordered-list" class="my-rem16px mx-0 pl-[1.25rem] list-disc marker:text-brandBlue-500 marker:pl-rem24px "><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Have trouble performing your daily routine.</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Notice ALS symptoms getting worse.</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Arent able to move around independently.</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Experience side effects from treatment.</li></ul><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">ALS can make breathing difficult. Symptoms of pulmonary (breathing) problems that indicate you should contact your provider include:</p><ul data-identity="unordered-list" class="my-rem16px mx-0 pl-[1.25rem] list-disc marker:text-brandBlue-500 marker:pl-rem24px "><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Shortness of breath, even during rest.</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Weak <a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/symptoms/17755-cough" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition">cough</a>.</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Difficulty clearing your throat and lungs.</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Extra saliva.</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Inability to lie flat in bed.</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Repeated chest infections (<a data-identity="link" href="https://my.clevelandclinic.org/health/diseases/4471-pneumonia" target="_blank" class="text-brandBlue-500 underline underline-offset-[5px] decoration-1 break-words hover:text-blue-800 transition">pneumonia</a>).</li></ul><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">These symptoms can lead to respiratory failure, where you arent breathing in enough oxygen to support your body. This is life-threatening. Contact emergency services if you have trouble breathing.</p><h3 data-identity="headline" class="text-gray-900 font-bold leading-rem30px text-rem25px bp600:text-rem32px bp600:leading-rem38px mt-rem32px mb-rem16px break-words ">What questions should I ask my healthcare provider?</h3><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">If you receive an ALS diagnosis, ask your provider:</p><ul data-identity="unordered-list" class="my-rem16px mx-0 pl-[1.25rem] list-disc marker:text-brandBlue-500 marker:pl-rem24px "><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">What treatments are available?</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">What medications can help?</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">What are the side effects of treatment?</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">How can I take care of myself?</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">What types of therapy will I need?</li><li class="mb-rem12px pl-rem12px text-gray-800 text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">What steps can I take now to slow the progression of the disease?</li></ul></div></div></div><h3 data-identity="headline" class="text-gray-900 font-bold leading-rem30px text-rem25px bp600:text-rem32px bp600:leading-rem38px mt-rem32px mb-rem16px">A note from Cleveland Clinic</h3><div data-identity="rich-text" class=""><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">Receiving an ALS (amyotrophic lateral sclerosis) diagnosis can spark a lot of questions and emotions. You may wonder, <em>What caused this and why?</em> You might even feel overwhelmed and frustrated by not being able to do routine things as well as you used to, like brushing your hair, enjoying a meal or maintaining a conversation with your loved ones. This can lead to depression and anxiety, especially as you start to see symptoms progressively get worse.</p><p data-identity="paragraph-element" class="text-gray-800 my-rem16px text-rem19px leading-rem34px ">No matter where you are or what youre feeling, your care team is available to help you. Treatment for ALS is improving, and new treatment options are being studied and tested at this very moment. While there isnt a current cure for ALS, treatment options can delay how fast symptoms progress and give you more time to spend with the people you care about.</p></div><div
